Done.


CLIP TIFF FILE


 command: gdalwarp -of GTiff -cutline "/home/klimplot/support/indonesia.shp" -cl indonesia -crop_to_cutline "/home/klimplot/data/2015.04.30_bulanan/ensMean.2015.05_ver_2015.04.30_full.tiff" "/home/klimplot/data/2015.04.30_bulanan/ensMean.2015.05_ver_2015.04.30.tiff"
